	<script>
		window.appBaseURI = 'https://'+window.location.host;
		window.informVwoExtension = function (data) {
			try {
				if (window.chrome && window.chrome.runtime && window.chrome.runtime.sendMessage) {
					window.chrome.runtime.sendMessage(window.vwoExtensionId, data);
				}
			} catch (e) {}
		};

		(function () {
			class Deferred {
				constructor() {
					this.promise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
						this.resolve = resolve;
						this.reject = reject;
					});
				}
			}
			let endpoint = '/login';
			const accountsEndpoint = '/user/accounts';
			// if(localStorage.getItem('lastDataRegionCacheKey')) {
			// 	const region = localStorage.getItem('lastDataRegionCacheKey');
			// 	endpoint = `/${region.toLowerCase()}${endpoint}`;
			// }
			const deferred = new Deferred();
			window.firstLoginCallPromise = deferred.promise;
			window.firstLoginCallPromise.catch(() => {
				delete window.firstLoginCallPromise;
			});
			var request = new XMLHttpRequest(),
				loginUrl = window.appBaseURI + endpoint,
				accountsUrl = window.appBaseURI + accountsEndpoint,
				searchParams = location.hash.split('?')[1] || '';
				//ignore searchParams for insightsDashboard
				if(searchParams.includes('insightsDashboard')){
					searchParams = ''
				}
			//Forward the search params in the login call.
			//Except for forget-password page. In this case we don't need to send the hash as it is sensitive information.
			if (searchParams && location.hash.indexOf('#/forgot-password') !==0) {
				loginUrl += '?' + searchParams;
				accountsUrl += '?' + searchParams;
			}
			request.withCredentials = true;
			request.open('GET', loginUrl, true);

			request.onerror = () => deferred.reject();
			request.onload = function() {
				if (request.status === 401) {
					if (location.protocol === 'http:') {
						location.protocol = 'https:';
						return;
					}
				}

				if(request.status === 200) {
					window.amILoggedIn = true;
					let data = JSON.parse(request.responseText);
					let accountsListPromise = fetch(accountsUrl).then(response => response.json());
					accountsListPromise.then((accountsList) => {
						data.accounts = accountsList;
						deferred.resolve(data);
					});
				} else {
					deferred.reject('Login call status: ' + request.status + ' ' + request.statusText);
				}
				// HACK: require only for local dev where login.js is fetched
				// through ajax
				var loginModuleCheckInterval = setInterval(function () {
					if (window.login) {
						clearInterval(loginModuleCheckInterval);
						login.init(request);
					}
				}, 50);
			};

			//if (location.protocol === 'http:') {
				request.send();
			//}
		})();

	</script>

	<script>
		(function () {
			var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
			window.loadCss = function loadCss(href) {
				var l = document.createElement('link');
				l.rel = 'stylesheet';
				// HACK: Trick to make styleheet not block rendering
				l.media = 'dummy';
				l.href = window.appBaseURI + "/" +href;
				head.appendChild(l);
				l.onload = function () {
					//HACK for FF41
					setTimeout(function (){
						l.media = 'all';
					},0);
				}
				return window;
			}

			window.loadCsses = function(cssList) {
				if(cssList) {
					if(Object.prototype.toString.call(cssList) === '[object Array]') {
						for(var i=0; i<cssList.length; i++) {
							loadCss(cssList[i]);
						}
					} else if(typeof cssList === 'string') {
						loadCss(cssList);
					}
				}

				return window;
			}
		})();

		window.loadCsses(csses.app);
		window.loadCsses(csses.iti);
	</script><link rel="stylesheet" media="all" href="https://app.vwo.com/styles/app.1a6a3665.css"><link rel="stylesheet" media="all" href="https://app.vwo.com/styles/iti.268450fc.css">

        signInHeading.innerHTML = 'Sign in to VWO platform';
    }
    function gotoOwnerAccountChangedView(isAccountOwnerUpdatedSuccessfully) {
        showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.accountOwnerUpdateViewSelector);
        if (isAccountOwnerUpdatedSuccessfully === 'false') {
            // in case of failure show failed icon and text respectively
            $('#owner-update-heading-sucess').hidden = true;
            document.getElementById('owner-update-success-notification-icon').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('owner-update-fail-notification-icon').style.display = 'inline-block';
            $('#owner-update-heading-failed').hidden = false;
            document.getElementById('owner-update-sub-heading').innerText = 'We are not able to process your request as the approval link is either invalid or it has expired.';
        }
    }
    /**
     * Sends an email to the email ID specified to reset the password.
     */
    function sendResetPasswordEmail() {
        var username = $('#forgot-password-username').value;
        xhr({
            method: 'POST',
            url: '/forgotPassword/sendcode',
            data: { username: username },
            onSuccess: function () {
                setNotification(messages.MSG_PASSWORD_RESET_MAIL_SENT.replace('%email%', username));
            },
            onFail: function (response) {
                setNotification(response.errors && response.errors[0].message || response.message);
            }
        });
    }
    /**
     * Sends a request to the server to verify if the password recovery hash is valid or not.
     */
    function verifyResetPasswordHash() {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
            xhr({
                method: 'GET',
                url: '/forgotPassword',
                data: 'hash=' + hash,
                onSuccess: resolve,
                onFail: reject
            });
        });
    }
    /**
     * Sends a reset password query to the server.`
     */
    function resetPassword() {
        var email = $('#js-login-confirm-email').value, newPassword = $('#js-login-new-password').value, confirmPassword = $('#js-login-confirm-password').value, form = $('#js-password-reset-form');
        var $scope = angular.element(form).scope();
        if (!$scope.resetPasswordForm.$valid) {
            setNotification(messages.FROM_INVALID);
            return;
        }
        if (newPassword !== confirmPassword) {
            setNotification(messages.MSG_PASSWORDS_DONT_MATCH);
            return;
        }
        setNotification();
        xhr({
            method: 'POST',
            url: '/forgotPassword/reset?hash=' + hash,
            data: { username: email, password: newPassword, confirmPassword: confirmPassword },
            onSuccess: function () {
                $scope.newPassword = '';
                showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.loginViewSelector);
                if (isSetPasswordState()) {
                    setNotification(messages.MSG_PASSWORD_SET_SUCCESS);
                }
                else {
                    setNotification(messages.MSG_PASSWORD_RESET_SUCCESS);
                }
                hideCaptcha();
            },
            onFail: function (response) {
                var msg = response.errors && response.errors[0].message || response.message;
                // HACK: ideally backend should send err code, but now we need to match exact message
                if (msg === 'Incorrect user input') {
                    msg = messages.MSG_EMAIL_WRONG;
                }
                setNotification(msg);
            }
        });
    }
    function showCaptcha(response) {
        if (response.showCaptcha) {
            captchaWrap.classList.remove('hidden');
            if (!window.grecaptcha) {
                var s = document.createElement('script');
                s.src = 'https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?onload=onloadRecaptchaCallback&render=explicit';
                document.head.appendChild(s);
                window.onloadRecaptchaCallback = function () {
                    window.grecaptcha.render('recaptcha-placeholder', {
                        'sitekey': response.captchaKey,
                        'callback': verifyRecaptchaCallback
                    });
                };
            }
            else {
                window.grecaptcha.reset();
            }
        }
        else {
            captchaResponse = '';
        }
    }
    function hideCaptcha() {
        captchaWrap.classList.add('hidden');
    }
    var verifyRecaptchaCallback = function (response) {
        captchaResponse = response;
    };
    function setNotification(message, notificationType) {
        if (message) {
            notificationBoxMsg.innerHTML = message;
            notificationBox.classList.remove('visibility--hidden');
            if (notificationType === NotificationType.INFO) {
                $('#js-notification-warning-icon').classList.add('hidden');
                $('#js-notification-info-icon').classList.remove('hidden');
                notificationBox.classList.add('notification-box--primary');
            }
            else {
                $('#js-notification-warning-icon').classList.remove('hidden');
                $('#js-notification-info-icon').classList.add('hidden');
                notificationBox.classList.remove('notification-box--primary');
            }
        }
        else {
            notificationBox.classList.add('visibility--hidden');
        }
    }
    function onLoginFail(response) {
        response = JSON.parse(response);
        if (response && !!response.isSsoEnabled) {
            goToSSOView();
            setNotification(messages.LOGIN_USING_SSO);
        }
        else {
            switch (response.message) {
                case 'Password Expired':
                    setNotification(messages.PASSWORD_EXPIRED);
                    break;
                case 'Inactive account':
                    setNotification(messages.DISABLED_ACCOUNT);
                    break;
                case 'Inactive User':
                    setNotification(messages.INACTIVE_USER);
                    break;
                case 'Deleted account':
                    setNotification(messages.ACCOUNT_DELETED);
                    break;
                default:
                    setNotification(messages.MSG_LOGIN_ERROR);
            }
        }
        showCaptcha(response);
    }
    function getRedirectionUrl(loggedInUser, injector) {

    function normalizeEndpointForRegion(endpoint, email) {

    function login(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        loginButton.classList.add('is-in-action');
        //Hide captcha and login messsage on login.
        captchaWrap.classList.add('hidden');
        setNotification();
        var request = new XMLHttpRequest(), loginUrl = window.appBaseURI +
            normalizeEndpointForRegion('/login', $('#login-username').value);
        request.withCredentials = true;
        request.open('POST', loginUrl, true);
        request.onload = function (data) {
            loginButton.classList.remove('is-in-action');
            // clear the credentials
            loginEmail = $('#login-username').value;
            $('#login-password').value = '';
            if (request.status === 200) {
                var response = JSON.parse(data.target.response);
                authToken = response['2FAAuthToken'];
                if ((response === null || response === void 0 ? void 0 : response.twoFactorAuthentication) === 'required') {
                    loginWith2FA(response.twoFactorAuthenticationMethod);
                }
                else {
                    onLoginSuccess(JSON.parse(data.target.response));
                }
            }
            else if (request.status === 401) {
                onLoginFail(request.responseText);
                loginEmail = '';
                // document.getElementById('login-container').removeAttribute("style");
            }
        };
        request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json;charset=UTF-8');
        var username = $('#login-username').value;
        var password = $('#login-password').value;
        var rememberMe = $('#checkbox-remember').checked;
        request.send(JSON.stringify({
            username: username,
            password: password,
            remember: rememberMe,
            recaptcha_response_field: captchaResponse // eslint-disable-line camelcase
        }));
    }
    function checkForInvalidSSOUser() {
        if (decodeURI(location.hash.split('#/sso?error=')[1]) === 'Invalid User') {
            setNotification(messages.INVALID_SSO_USER);
        }
        else if (location.hash.includes('#/sso?error=')) {
            setNotification(messages.UNEXPECTED_ERROR);
        }
    }
    function onLoginSuccess(data) {
        var currentLoginDetails = {
            email: data.email,
            state: currentLoginState
        };
        localStorage.setItem(loginDetailsKey, JSON.stringify(currentLoginDetails));
        var metaTag = document.getElementById('meta-viewport');
        metaTag.content = 'width=1280';
        window.amILoggedIn = true;
        loginWrap.classList.add('hidden');
        window.localStorage.setItem('isCachedLoad', '1');
        var loginStyleTag = document.querySelector('#login-style');
        if (loginStyleTag) {
            document.head.removeChild(loginStyleTag);
        }
        var loggedInUser = data;
        var accountsListPromise = fetch('user/accounts').then(function (response) { return response.json(); });
        waitForDeps(loggedInUser).then(function (_a) {
            var aMsgHandlerService = _a.aMsgHandlerService, redirectTo = _a.redirectTo;
            var injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
            var MultiTabsUtils = injector.get('MultiTabsUtils');
            MultiTabsUtils.broadcast('AppLoggedIn'); // can't import enum
            var commonAnalyticsUtils = injector.get('commonAnalyticsUtils');
            var SegmentAnalyticsEnum = injector.get('SegmentAnalyticsEnum');
            commonAnalyticsUtils.trackSegmentOnNextLoad(SegmentAnalyticsEnum.COMMON.APP_LOGGED_IN);
            accountsListPromise.then(function (accountsList) {
                loggedInUser.accounts = accountsList;
                aMsgHandlerService.setLoginDetails(loggedInUser);
                location.hash = redirectTo;
                // Get back the loading bar
                loadingBarStyleTag === null || loadingBarStyleTag === void 0 ? void 0 : loadingBarStyleTag.remove();
            });
        });
        document.getElementById('js-main-container-wrap').classList.add('login-successful');
    }

    function onStateSuccess() {
        var _a;
        var matchHash = location.hash.match(/hash=(.*)/);
        // check if account owner is changed
        var isAccountOwnerUpdatedSuccessfully = window.localStorage.getItem('accountOwnerUpdateStatus');
        if (location.hash.match(/forgot-password|set-password/)) {
            showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.forgotPasswordViewSelector);
        }
        else if (location.hash.match(/sso/)) {
            showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.ssoViewSelector);
            checkForInvalidSSOUser();
            signInHeading.innerHTML = 'Sign in to VWO platform using SSO';
        }
        else if (isAccountOwnerUpdatedSuccessfully) {
            window.localStorage.removeItem('accountOwnerUpdateStatus');
            gotoOwnerAccountChangedView(isAccountOwnerUpdatedSuccessfully);
        }
        else if (!location.hash.match(/marketing_test_banner=\d/)) {
            gotoLoginView();
        }
        if (matchHash) {
            hash = matchHash[1];
            (_a = $('#js-forgot-password-loader')) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.classList.remove('hidden');
            Promise.all([
                verifyResetPasswordHash(),
                waitForAngular()
            ]).then(function () {
                showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.resetPasswordViewSelector);
                if (isSetPasswordState()) {
                    $('#js-password-reset-form-only-button').classList.remove('hidden');
                    setNotification(messages.SET_PASSWORD_MAIL_FOLLOWUP);
                    var email = atob(decodeURIComponent(location.hash.split('email=')[1]));
                    $('#js-login-confirm-email').value = email;
                    $('#js-login-confirm-email').setAttribute('disabled', true);
                }
                else {
                    $('#js-password-reset-form-button-with-back').classList.remove('hidden');
                    setNotification(messages.MSG_PASSWORD_RESET_MAIL_FOLLOWUP);
                    var email = atob(decodeURIComponent(location.hash.split('email=')[1]));
                    if (email) {
                        $('#js-login-confirm-email').value = email;
                        $('#js-login-confirm-email').setAttribute('disabled', true);
                    }
                }
            }).catch(function (response) {
                var msg;
                if (isSetPasswordState()) {
                    if (response.errors && response.errors[0].message === 'linkRevoked') {
                        msg = messages.MSG_USER_REVOKED;
                    }
                    else {
                        msg = messages.MSG_PASSWORD_INVITE_MAIL_EXPIRED;
                    }
                }
                else {
                    msg = messages.MSG_PASSWORD_RESET_MAIL_EXPIRED;
                }
                setTimeout(function () {
                    setNotification(msg);
                });
                // Unhide the forgot password form hidden because of hash in url
                showFormBlock(FormBlockSelectors.forgotPasswordViewSelector);
                hash = '';
                gotoLoginView();
            })
                .finally(function () {
                var _a;
                (_a = $('#js-forgot-password-loader')) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.remove();
            });
        }
    }
    function isSetPasswordState() {
        return location.hash.match(/set-password/);
    }
    function showInitLoginMessage() {
        // Show message as directed by a temporary cookie sent by backend.
        // The set of expected values is : { 'MSG_EMAIL_WRONG', 'RESET', 'REVERIFY', 'ALREADY_VERIFIED', 'DISABLED'}
        // @ts-expect-error
        var cookieValue = document.getCookie(initMessageCookieName);
        if (cookieValue) {
            setNotification(messages[cookieValue]);
        }
    }
    function getLoginBannerConfig() {
        var currURL = window.location.href;
        var apiURL = '/marketing/login-page-content';
        var isTestingMode = currURL.indexOf('marketing_test_banner') !== -1;
        var queryParams = isTestingMode ? '?post_config=local' : '';
        return fetch(apiURL + queryParams)
            .then(function (response) { return response.json(); })
            .then(function (data) {
            if (isTestingMode) {
                var templateID_1 = parseInt(currURL.split('=')[1]);
                return data.find(function (obj) { return obj.id === templateID_1; });
            }
            if (data.length === 0) {
                return fallbackResponse;
            }
            var templateIndx = parseInt(String(Math.random() * data.length));
            return data[templateIndx];
        })
            .catch(function (e) {
            return fallbackResponse;
        });
    }
    function renderLoginBanner() {

                            onmouseenter: function () { return elem.style.backgroundColor = obj.hoverColor; },
                            onmouseleave: function () { return elem.style.backgroundColor = obj.color; }
                        });
                        elem.style.cssText = "color: ".concat(obj.textColor, "; background-color: ").concat(obj.color);
                    }

    /**
     * Shows login box and processes URL if required. Called after initial login verification
     * from index.html.
     * @param  {Boolean | Object} param If boolean informs whether user is logged in.
     *				If object, it serves as response from the login request.
     */
    function init(param) {
        var _a, _b;
        return __awaiter(this, void 0, void 0, function () {

                            isLoggedIn = param;
                        }
                        else {

                            response = (param && param.responseText !== '' && JSON.parse(param.responseText));
                        }
                        if (!!isLoggedIn) return [3 /*break*/, 2];
                        document.title = 'Login - VWO';
                        metaTag.content = 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1';
                        if (response) {
                            showCaptcha(response);
                        }
                        document.getElementById('js-main-container-wrap').classList.remove('login-successful');
                        loginWrap.classList.remove('hidden');
                        // Hide the top loading bar while we are logged out
                        if (!document.getElementById('loading-bar-style-tag')) {
                            loadingBarStyleTag = document.createElement('style');
                            loadingBarStyleTag.id = 'loading-bar-style-tag';
                            loadingBarStyleTag.textContent = '#loading-bar { display: none!important; }';
                            document.head.appendChild(loadingBarStyleTag);
                        }

                            goToSSOView();
                        }
                        onStateSuccess();
                        showInitLoginMessage();
                        return [4 /*yield*/, waitForAngular()];

                            setNotification('Please login to enable new campaign creation flow.', NotificationType.INFO);
                        }

                        metaTag.content = 'width=1280';

                        if (!(!hasToken &&
                            ((_b = response.currentAccount) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.onboarding) &&
                            response.currentAccount.onboarding.version === 2 &&

                        return [3 /*break*/, 5];

                            response.currentAccount.shouldSeeVWOSetup &&
                            !response.currentAccount.isExpired &&
                            (response.policy.ruleset.isAdmin || response.policy.ruleset.canPublish)) {
                            location.hash = '/setup/account-setup';
                        }
                        else if (!hasToken && window.location.hash.split('?')[0] === '#/login') {

    // Check if this is not a cached load, fallback to system font so that login doesn't have to wait for the main fonts to load and neither sees a flicker on login
    if (!window.localStorage || !window.localStorage.getItem('isCachedLoad')) {

    function waitForAngular() {
        return new Promise(function (resolve) {
            if (window.angular) {
                try {
                    window.angular.module('vwo');
                    resolve(undefined);
                    return;
                }
                catch (e) {
                    // ignore module not found error and wait more
                }
            }
            setTimeout(function () {
                waitForAngular().then(resolve);
            }, 200);
        });
    }
    function loginWith2FA(authMode) {
        waitForAngular().then(function () {
            var $injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
            var $rootScope = $injector.get('$rootScope');
            $rootScope.loginScreen = {
                loginEmail: loginEmail,
                isOTPScreenVisible: true,
                isTotpAuthRequired: authMode === 'totp',
                resendBtnTimer: 20,
                generateOTP: generateOTP,
                loginWithOtp: loginWithOtp,
                hideOtpScreen: function () {
                    $rootScope.loginScreen.isOTPScreenVisible = false;
                },
                retryInterval: undefined
            };
            if (!$rootScope.loginScreen.isTotpAuthRequired) {
                generateOTP();
            }
        });
    }
    function loginWithOtp() {
        var $injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
        var $http = $injector.get('$http');
        var $rootScope = $injector.get('$rootScope');
        $rootScope.loginScreen.showLoader = true;
        setNotification();
        $http({
            url: window.appBaseURI + '/login/authToken',
            method: 'POST',
            data: {
                action: $rootScope.loginScreen.isTotpAuthRequired ? '2FA-totp-verify' : '2FA-login',
                accessToken: $rootScope.loginScreen.otp,
                '2FAAuthToken': authToken
            }
        }).then(function (response) {
            $rootScope.loginScreen.showLoader = false;
            onLoginSuccess(response.data);
        }).catch(function (response) {
            var _a, _b, _c, _d;
            $rootScope.loginScreen.showLoader = false;
            if (response.status === 401) {
                $rootScope.loginScreen.hideOtpScreen();
            }
            else {
                if (((_c = (_b = (_a = response.data.errors) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a[0]) === null || _b === void 0 ? void 0 : _b.data) === null || _c === void 0 ? void 0 : _c.errMsg) === 'MAX_LIMIT_REACHED') {
                    $rootScope.loginScreen.isMaxLimitReached = true;
                    $rootScope.loginScreen.otp = '';
                    if ($rootScope.loginScreen.isTotpAuthRequired) {
                        $rootScope.loginScreen.resendBtnTimer = (_d = response.data.errors[0].data.remTimer) !== null && _d !== void 0 ? _d : 60;
                        setRetryCodeTimer($rootScope.loginScreen.resendBtnTimer);
                    }
                }
                else {
                    setNotification(response.data.errors[0].message);
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function generateOTP() {
        var $injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
        var $http = $injector.get('$http');
        var $rootScope = $injector.get('$rootScope');
        $rootScope.loginScreen.isMaxLimitReached = false;
        setNotification();
        $rootScope.loginScreen.disableResend = true;
        $http({
            url: window.appBaseURI + '/account/access-token/send/login',
            method: 'POST',
            data: {
                action: '2FA-login',
                '2FAAuthToken': authToken
            }
        }).then(function (data) {
            $rootScope.loginScreen.disableResend = false;
            setRetryCodeTimer(20);
        }).catch(function (e) {
            if (e.status === 401) {
                $rootScope.loginScreen.hideOtpScreen();
            }
            else {
                $rootScope.loginScreen.disableResend = false;
                setNotification(e.data.errors[0].message);
            }
        });
    }
    function shouldRedirectToExplore(account) {
        var _a;
        return __awaiter(this, void 0, void 0, function () {
            var $injector, $rootScope, exploreService, campaignUtils, CampaignResource, _b;
            return __generator(this, function (_c) {
                switch (_c.label) {
                    case 0:
                        if (((_a = account === null || account === void 0 ? void 0 : account.onboarding) === null || _a === void 0 ? void 0 : _a.version) !== 3) {
                            return [2 /*return*/, false];
                        }
                        return [4 /*yield*/, waitForAngular()];
                    case 1:
                        _c.sent();
                        $injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
                        $rootScope = $injector.get('$rootScope');
                        exploreService = $injector.get('exploreService');
                        campaignUtils = $injector.get('campaignUtils');
                        CampaignResource = $injector.get('CampaignResource');
                        _b = $rootScope.campaignsCount;
                        if (_b) return [3 /*break*/, 3];
                        return [4 /*yield*/, CampaignResource.queryCampaignsCount().then(function (campaignsCount) {
                                $rootScope.campaignsCount = campaignsCount;
                                return campaignsCount;
                            })];
                    case 2:
                        _b = (_c.sent());
                        _c.label = 3;
                    case 3:
                        _b;
                        if (campaignUtils.getCreatedCampaignCountAcrossProducts() === 0 &&
                            !exploreService.isExploreScreenVisited()) {
                            return [2 /*return*/, true];
                        }
                        else {
                            return [2 /*return*/, false];
                        }
                        return [2 /*return*/];
                }
            });
        });
    }
    function setRetryCodeTimer(timer) {
        var $injector = angular.element(document.body).injector();
        var $interval = $injector.get('$interval');
        var $rootScope = $injector.get('$rootScope');
        $interval.cancel($rootScope.loginScreen.retryInterval);
        $rootScope.loginScreen.resendBtnTimer = timer;
        $rootScope.loginScreen.retryInterval = $interval(function () {
            if (!($rootScope === null || $rootScope === void 0 ? void 0 : $rootScope.loginScreen.resendBtnTimer)) {
                if ($rootScope.loginScreen.isTotpAuthRequired) {
                    $rootScope.loginScreen.isMaxLimitReached = false;
                }
                $interval.cancel($rootScope.loginScreen.retryInterval);
            }
            $rootScope.loginScreen.resendBtnTimer--;
        }, 1000);
    }
    window.login = {
        gotoForgotPasswordView: gotoForgotPasswordView,
        gotoLoginView: function () {
            gotoLoginView();
        },
        login: login,
        init: init,
        sendResetPasswordEmail: sendResetPasswordEmail,

@ts-strict-ignore
// DO NOT USE IMPORTS IN THIS FILE. THIS FILE IS LOADED WITHOUT REQUIREJS
(function () {
    'use strict';
    var ready = false;
    var readyState = 0; //0 for not loaded, 1 for loaded, -1 for error
    var instance;
    var subscribers = {
        onLoad: [],
        onError: []
    };
    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = '; ' + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split('; ' + name + '=');
        if (parts.length === 2) {
            return parts.pop().split(';').shift();
        }
    }
    function getEnv() {
        var env = '';
        if (location.hostname === 'app.vwo.com') {
            env = 'production';
        }
        else if (location.hostname.indexOf('staging') >= 0) {
            env = 'staging';
        }
        else {
            env = 'development';
        }
        return env;
    }
    function isReady() {
        return ready;
    }
    //Runs the handler passed when the translator has been set.
    //In case the translator isn't ready it queues them
    //and waits otherwise immediately runs.
    function onLoad(handler) {
        if (readyState === 1) {
            handler();
        }
        else {
            subscribers.onLoad.push(handler);
        }
    }
    //Same as onLoad handler.
    function onError(handler) {
        if (readyState === -1) {
            handler();
        }
        else {
            subscribers.onError.push(handler);
        }
    }
    function setTranslator(transifexLive) {
        if (instance) {
            return;
        }
        // Hack - run transifexReadyHandler which we captured while fetching live.js. Code in index.html
        window.transifexReadyHandlers.forEach(function (handler) {
            handler();
        });
        //window.disableTranslation = true;
        instance = transifexLive;
        ready = true;
    }
    function getInstance() {
        return instance;
    }
    window.liveSettings = {
        'api_key': '1d1ede8d55354b0790713b1a9dab51d9',
        'picker': 'bottom-right',
        'parse_attr': [
            'data-nav-tooltip-subtext',
            'data-nav-tooltip',
            'vwo-dynamic-translate',
            'title'
        ],
        'detectlang': function () {
            return getCookie('lang') ? getCookie('lang') : 'en';
        },
        'ignore_class': ['graph-container'],
        'dynamic': false,
        // for development purposes please set autocollect to 'true' or set the enviroment as 'development'
        'autocollect': getEnv() === 'staging' ? true : false,
        'staging': getEnv() !== 'production' ? true : false
    };
    if (getCookie('lang') && getCookie('lang') !== 'en') {
        var liveScript = document.createElement('script');
        liveScript.src = '//d5phz18u4wuww.cloudfront.net/live.js';
        liveScript.type = 'text/javascript';
        document.head.appendChild(liveScript);
        liveScript.onload = function () {
            if (window.Transifex) {
                // Following hack to force get the languages from transifex.
                var jsonpUrl_1 = getEnv() === 'production' ? 'languages.jsonp' : 'languages.staging.jsonp';
                var loadScript_1 = window.Transifex.live.loadScript;
                window.Transifex.live.loadScript = function (url, callback) {
                    if (url.includes(jsonpUrl_1)) {
                        url = url.replace(jsonpUrl_1, jsonpUrl_1 + '?v=29');
                    }
                    return loadScript_1.call(window.Transifex.live, url, callback);
                };
                setTranslator(window.Transifex.live);
                subscribers.onLoad.forEach(function (handler) {
                    handler();
                });
                readyState = 1;
            }
            else {
                subscribers.onError.forEach(function (handler) {
                    handler();
                });
                readyState = -1;
            }
        };
        liveScript.onError = function () {
            subscribers.onError.forEach(function (handler) {
                handler();
            });
            readyState = -1;
        };
    }
    else {
        subscribers.onError.forEach(function (handler) {
            handler();
        });
        readyState = -1;
    }
    function jsonp(url) {
        var script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = url;
        document.body.appendChild(script);
        return function () { return document.body.removeChild(script); };
    }
    window.translatorSettings = {
        setTranslator: setTranslator,
        isReady: isReady,
        getInstance: getInstance,
        onLoad: onLoad,
        onError: onError
    };
})();
